                  productQtys.push({\n                        'id' : $(element).readAttribute('data-cart-item-id'),\n                        'qty' : $(element).getValue()\n                    });\n                });\n                this.productQtys = productQtys;\n            },\n            collectMiniCartQtys : function() {\n                var productQtys = [];\n                $$('input[data-cart-item-id]').each(function(element){\n                    productQtys.push({\n                        'id' : $(element).readAttribute('data-cart-item-id'),\n                        'qty' : $(element).getValue()\n                    });\n                });\n                this.productQtys = productQtys;\n            },\n            collectProductsForMessages : function() {\n                this.addedProducts = [];\n                this.removedProducts = [];\n                for (var i = 0; i < this.productWithChanges.length; i++) {\n                    var product = this.productWithChanges[i];\n                    if (typeof(this.origProducts[product.id]) != 'undefined') {\n                        if (product.qty > this.origProducts[product.id].qty) {\n                            product.qty = Math.abs(product.qty - this.origProducts[product.id].qty);\n                            this.addedProducts.push(product);\n                        } else if (product.qty < this.origProducts[product.id].qty) {\n                            product.qty = Math.abs(this.origProducts[product.id].qty - product.qty);\n                            this.removedProducts.push(product);\n                        }\n                    }\n                }\n            },\n            formatProductsArray : function(productsIn) {\n                var productsOut = [];\n                var itemId;\n                for (var i in productsIn)\n                {\n                    if (i != 'length' && productsIn.hasOwnProperty(i)) {\n                        if (typeof(productsIn[i]['sku']) != 'undefined') {\n                            itemId = productsIn[i].sku;\n                        } else {\n                            itemId = productsIn[i].id;\n                        }\n                        productsOut.push({\n                            'id': itemId,\n                            'name': productsIn[i].name,\n                            'price': productsIn[i].price,\n                            'quantity': parseInt(productsIn[i].qty, 10)\n                        });\n                    }\n                }\n                return productsOut;\n            },\n            cartItemAdded : function() {\n                if (this.addedProducts.length == 0) {\n                    return;\n                }\n                dataLayer.push({\n                    'event': 'addToCart',\n                    'ecommerce': {\n                        'currencyCode' : dlCurrencyCode,\n                        'add': {\n                            'products': this.formatProductsArray(this.addedProducts)\n                        }\n                    }\n                });\n                this.addedProducts = [];\n            },\n            cartItemRemoved : function() {\n                if (this.removedProducts.length == 0) {\n                    return;\n                }\n                dataLayer.push({\n                    'event': 'removeFromCart',\n                    'ecommerce': {\n                        'currencyCode' : dlCurrencyCode,\n                        'remove': {\n                            'products': this.formatProductsArray(this.removedProducts)\n                        }\n                    }\n                });\n                this.removedProducts = [];\n            },\n            parseAddToCartCookies : function(){\n                if(getCookie(cookieAddToCart)){\n                    this.addedProducts = [];\n                    var addProductsList = decodeURIComponent(getCookie(cookieAddToCart));\n                    this.addedProducts = JSON.parse(addProductsList);\n                    delCookie(cookieAddToCart);\n                    this.cartItemAdded();\n                }\n            },\n            parseRemoveFromCartCookies : function(){\n                if(getCookie(cookieRemoveFromCart)){\n                    this.removedProducts = [];\n                    var removeProductsList = decodeURIComponent(getCookie(cookieRemoveFromCart));\n                    this.removedProducts = JSON.parse(removeProductsList);\n                    delCookie(cookieRemoveFromCart);\n                    this.cartItemRemoved();\n                }\n            }\n        };\n\n        var googleAnalyticsUniversal = new GoogleAnalyticsUniversal();\n        var googleAnalyticsUniversalCart = new GoogleAnalyticsUniversalCart();\n\n        document.observe('dom:loaded', function() {\n            googleAnalyticsUniversal.updatePromotions();\n            googleAnalyticsUniversal.updateImpressions();\n            googleAnalyticsUniversalCart.parseAddToCartCookies();\n            googleAnalyticsUniversalCart.parseRemoveFromCartCookies();\n            googleAnalyticsUniversalCart.subscribeProductsUpdateInCart();\n            googleAnalyticsUniversalCart.listenMinicartReload();\n            dataLayer.push({'ecommerce':{'impressions':0,'promoView':0}});\n        });\n\n        function getCookie(name) {\n            var cookie = \" \" + document.cookie;\n            var search = \" \" + name + \"=\";\n            var setStr = null;\n            var offset = 0;\n            var end = 0;\n            if (cookie.length > 0) {\n                offset = cookie.indexOf(search);\n                if (offset != -1) {\n                    offset += search.length;\n                    end = cookie.indexOf(\";\", offset);\n                    if (end == -1) {\n                        end = cookie.length;\n                    }\n                    setStr = decodeURI(cookie.substring(offset, end));\n                }\n            }\n            return(setStr);\n        }\n\n        function delCookie(name) {\n            var date = new Date(0);\n            var cookie = name + \"=\" + \"; path=/; expires=\" + date.toUTCString();\n            document.cookie = cookie;\n        }\n    });\n</script>\n\n\n\n<script type=\"text/javascript\">\n    requirejs(['jquery', 'jquery/jquery.cookie', 'domReady!'], personal electronic cutter has changed the face of crafting and scrapbooking. While it has many uses, one of the most popular is&nbsp;<a class=\"graylink\" href=\"videos\">cutting vinyl.</a></p>\n<p>Expressions Vinyl sells craft vinyl for all your scrapbook vinyl and vinyl crafting needs.</p>\n<p>We sell the same craft vinyl that Provo Craft sells for their Cricut vinyl. We cut out the fancy Cricut vinyl packaging and the distribution system to bring the same high quality Cricut vinyl to you at a fraction the cost.</p>\n<h3>Save Money On Cricut Vinyl</h3>\n<p><strong>Don't pay $5 a sheet</strong>&nbsp;for Cricut vinyl. We sell the same craft vinyl material for the everday&nbsp;<strong>low price of $1.99</strong>&nbsp;a sheet. You also don't have to buy two sheets of the same color if you don't want to. We sell them individually,&nbsp;<strong>12\"x24\" for just $1.99</strong>.</p>\n<p>Our Cricut vinyl is available in a variety of sizes and colors. We also sell&nbsp;<a title=\"Transfer Tape\" href=\"transfer-tape.html\" target=\"_blank\">transfer tape</a>, so you can finish your projects!</p>\n<h3>Special Offers!</h3>\n<p>Don't forget to register for our special offers and save even more! Subscribers receive emails about new craft vinyl project ideas and updates about new products as well as receive coupon codes.</p>\n<p>We&nbsp;<strong>never spam</strong>&nbsp;and&nbsp;<strong>never sell or give</strong>&nbsp;your email address to anyone.</p>\n<h3>Our Craft Vinyl Works With -</h3>\n<ul>\n<li>Cricut machines</li>\n<li>Silhouette Cameo, Curio and Portrait Cutting Machines</li>\n<li>Graphtec - Craft ROBO</li>\n<li>Quickutz - Sillhouette</li>\n<li>Pazzles - Inspiration</li>\n<li>Xyron - Wishblade</li>\n<li>Any other cutter/plotter</li>\n</ul>\n<div>\n<h3>What Is Cricut Vinyl?</h3>\n<p>Vinyl is a highly versatile PVC film product that is well suited to crafting, decorating, and scrap booking.&nbsp; This vinyl film has a pressure sensitive adhesive layer on the back that will allow it to adhere to many surfaces from smooth to semi rough.</p>\n<p>Expressions Vinyl currently carries two different types of vinyl.&nbsp; The first which we call “Cricut Vinyl” is made by Oracal.&nbsp; This particular vinyl is&nbsp;<a title=\"Cricut Vinyl Specs\" href=\"specs.html\" target=\"_blank\">Oracal 631</a>&nbsp;and is the exact same product Provo Craft sells for their popular Cricut machines.&nbsp; This Cricut vinyl is compatible with any electronic craft cutter, not just the Cricut.&nbsp; We also carry a product we call “Outdoor Cricut Vinyl”.&nbsp; This product is&nbsp;<a title=\"Cricut Vinyl Specs\" href=\"specs.html\" target=\"_blank\">Oracal 651</a>&nbsp;and is similar to the “Cricut Vinyl”, but is better suited for outdoor applications.</p>\n<p>Our vinyl is available in thirty colors and we are so confident you will love our vinyl we stand behind it with a full&nbsp;<a title=\"Expressions Vinyl Satisfaction Guarentee\" href=\"about-us.html\" target=\"_blank\">satisfaction guarantee</a>.&nbsp; We also want to make sure you know how to use your Cricut vinyl, we have&nbsp;<a title=\"Cricut Vinyl Videos\" href=\"videos\">How-To Videos</a>.&nbsp; We also have&nbsp;<a title=\"Cricut Vinyl Project Ideas\" href=\"project-ideas.html\" target=\"_blank\">Project Ideas</a>&nbsp;to make sure you never run out of ideas for your Cricut vinyl.</p>\n<h3>Vinyl For Cricut</h3>\n<p>We sell a few different types of vinyl for Cricut. First there is&nbsp;<a title=\"Oracal 631 Removable Indoor Vinyl\" href=\"adhesive-vinyl/removable-indoor-vinyl.html\" target=\"_blank\">\"Cricut Vinyl\"</a>&nbsp;which is Oracal 631. This is the same stuff that Provo Craft sells. We also have&nbsp;<a title=\"Oracal 651 Permanent Outdoor Vinyl\" href=\"adhesive-vinyl/permanent-outdoor-vinyl.html\" target=\"_blank\">\"Outdoor Cricut Vinyl\"</a>&nbsp;which is Oracal 651. This is similar to the \"Cricut Vinyl\", but has a gloss finish and a more aggressive adhesive.</p>\n<p>Then there is&nbsp;<a title=\"Siser Heat Transfer Vinyl\" href=\"heat-transfer-vinyl.html\" target=\"_blank\">heat transfer vinyl</a>&nbsp;for Cricut. This is used for making vinyl graphics that transfer onto fabric.</p>\n<p>Lastly is our newwest vinyl. We now have&nbsp;<a title=\"Patterned Adhesive Vinyl\" href=\"adhesive-vinyl/patterned-adhesive-vinyl.html\" target=\"_blank\">patterned vinyl</a>, such as zebra pring, houndstooth,&nbsp;damask, and polka dot.</p>\n<h3>Add A Button To Your Blog!</h3>\n<p>Share the great Cricut vinyl deals with all your friends with an ExpressionsVinyl.com button on your blog.
